I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
task --resume-last ignores current-session scoping and can resume another Claude session's task
## Summary

`task-resume-candidate --json` is scoped to the current Claude session, but `task --resume-last` is not. In a multi-session workspace, the CLI can report that there is no resumable task for the current session and then still resume a different session's persisted Codex thread.

The same helper also lets an active task from another Claude session block `--resume-last`, even when `/codex:status` for the current session shows no running jobs.

## Reproduction

1. Start a repository with the plugin state directory available.
2. Run one successful `task` command under Claude session `sess-other` so it persists a completed task thread.
3. In a separate Claude session `sess-current`, run:
   - `node scripts/codex-companion.mjs task-resume-candidate --json`
   - `node scripts/codex-companion.mjs task --resume-last "follow up"`
4. Observe that `task-resume-candidate` reports `available: false`, but `--resume-last` still resumes the older thread from `sess-other`.
5. Alternatively, leave a `running` task owned by `sess-other` in state and run `task --resume-last` from `sess-current`.

## Expected

- Implicit resume selection should use the same current-session visibility rules as `task-resume-candidate`.
- If `CODEX_COMPANION_SESSION_ID` is set and the current session has no resumable task, `task --resume-last` should fail with "No previous Codex task thread was found for this repository.".
- A running task from another session should not block `--resume-last` for the current session.

## Actual

- `task-resume-candidate` says there is no resumable task in the current session.
- `task --resume-last` still resumes another session's completed thread.
- A running task from another session can also block `--resume-last` with `Task ... is still running. Use /codex:status before continuing it.` even though `/codex:status` for the current session shows no running jobs.

## Suspected Cause

`resolveLatestTrackedTaskThread(...)` scans all persisted task jobs in the workspace and only excludes the current job id. It does not apply current-session filtering before choosing a completed thread or before checking for active tasks.

## Suggested Fix

Thread the same session-aware filtering used by `task-resume-candidate` into the implicit `--resume-last` path, and only fall back to `findLatestTaskThread(...)` when there is no Claude session id in scope.


</pr_description>

    79	      "  node scripts/codex-companion.mjs adversarial-review [--wait|--background] [--base <ref>] [--scope <auto|working-tree|branch>] [focus text]",
    80	      "  node scripts/codex-companion.mjs task [--background] [--write] [--resume-last|--resume|--fresh] [--model <model|spark>] [--effort <none|minimal|low|medium|high|xhigh>] [prompt]",
    81	      "  node scripts/codex-companion.mjs status [job-id] [--all] [--json]",
    82	      "  node scripts/codex-companion.mjs result [job-id] [--json]",
    83	      "  node scripts/codex-companion.mjs cancel [job-id] [--json]"
    84	    ].join("\n")
    85	  );
    86	}
    87	
    88	function outputResult(value, asJson) {
    89	  if (asJson) {
    90	    console.log(JSON.stringify(value, null, 2));
    91	  } else {
    92	    process.stdout.write(value);
    93	  }
    94	}
    95	
    96	function outputCommandResult(payload, rendered, asJson) {
    97	  outputResult(asJson ? payload : rendered, asJson);
    98	}
    99	
   100	function normalizeRequestedModel(model) {
   101	  if (model == null) {
   102	    return null;
   103	  }
   104	  const normalized = String(model).trim();
   105	  if (!normalized) {
   106	    return null;
   107	  }
   108	  return MODEL_ALIASES.get(normalized.toLowerCase()) ?? normalized;
   109	}
   110	
   111	function normalizeReasoningEffort(effort) {
   112	  if (effort == null) {
   113	    return null;
   114	  }
   115	  const normalized = String(effort).trim().toLowerCase();
   116	  if (!normalized) {
   117	    return null;
   118	  }
   119	  if (!VALID_REASONING_EFFORTS.has(normalized)) {
   120	    throw new Error(
   121	      `Unsupported reasoning effort "${effort}". Use one of: none, minimal, low, medium, high, xhigh.`
   122	    );
   123	  }
   124	  return normalized;
   125	}
   126	
   127	function normalizeArgv(argv) {
   128	  if (argv.length === 1) {
   129	    const [raw] = argv;
   130	    if (!raw || !raw.trim()) {
   131	      return [];
   132	    }
   133	    return splitRawArgumentString(raw);
   134	  }
   135	  return argv;
   136	}
   137	
   138	function parseCommandInput(argv, config = {}) {
   139	  return parseArgs(normalizeArgv(argv), {
   140	    ...config,
   141	    aliasMap: {
   142	      C: "cwd",
   143	      ...(config.aliasMap ?? {})
   144	    }
   145	  });
   146	}
   147	
   148	function resolveCommandCwd(options = {}) {
   149	  return options.cwd ? path.resolve(process.cwd(), options.cwd) : process.cwd();
   150	}
   151	
   152	function resolveCommandWorkspace(options = {}) {
   153	  return resolveWorkspaceRoot(resolveCommandCwd(options));
   154	}
   155	
   156	function sleep(ms) {
   157	  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
   158	}
   159	
   160	function shorten(text, limit = 96) {
   161	  const normalized = String(text ?? "").trim().replace(/\s+/g, " ");
   162	  if (!normalized) {
   163	    return "";
   164	  }
   165	  if (normalized.length <= limit) {
   166	    return normalized;
   167	  }
   168	  return `${normalized.slice(0, limit - 3)}...`;
   169	}
   170	
   171	function firstMeaningfulLine(text, fallback) {
   172	  const line = String(text ?? "")
   173	    .split(/\r?\n/)
   174	    .map((value) => value.trim())
   175	    .find(Boolean);
   176	  return line ?? fallback;
   177	}
   178	
   179	function buildSetupReport(cwd, actionsTaken = []) {
   180	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   181	  const nodeStatus = binaryAvailable("node", ["--version"], { cwd });
   182	  const npmStatus = binaryAvailable("npm", ["--version"], { cwd });
   183	  const codexStatus = getCodexAvailability(cwd);
   184	  const authStatus = getCodexLoginStatus(cwd);
   185	  const config = getConfig(workspaceRoot);
   186	
   187	  const nextSteps = [];
   188	  if (!codexStatus.available) {
   189	    nextSteps.push("Install Codex with `npm install -g @openai/codex`.");
   190	  }
   191	  if (codexStatus.available && !authStatus.loggedIn) {
   192	    nextSteps.push("Run `!codex login`.");
   193	    nextSteps.push("If browser login is blocked, retry with `!codex login --device-auth` or `!codex login --with-api-key`.");
   194	  }
   195	  if (!config.stopReviewGate) {
   196	    nextSteps.push("Optional: run `/codex:setup --enable-review-gate` to require a fresh review before stop.");
   197	  }
   198	
   199	  return {
   200	    ready: nodeStatus.available && codexStatus.available && authStatus.loggedIn,
   201	    node: nodeStatus,
   202	    npm: npmStatus,
   203	    codex: codexStatus,
   204	    auth: authStatus,
   205	    sessionRuntime: getSessionRuntimeStatus(),
   206	    reviewGateEnabled: Boolean(config.stopReviewGate),
   207	    actionsTaken,
   208	    nextSteps
   209	  };
   210	}
   211	
   212	function handleSetup(argv) {
   213	  const { options } = parseCommandInput(argv, {
   214	    valueOptions: ["cwd"],
   215	    booleanOptions: ["json", "enable-review-gate", "disable-review-gate"]
   216	  });
   217	
   218	  if (options["enable-review-gate"] && options["disable-review-gate"]) {
   219	    throw new Error("Choose either --enable-review-gate or --disable-review-gate.");
   220	  }
   221	
   222	  const cwd = resolveCommandCwd(options);
   223	  const workspaceRoot = resolveCommandWorkspace(options);
   224	  const actionsTaken = [];
   225	
   226	  if (options["enable-review-gate"]) {
   227	    setConfig(workspaceRoot, "stopReviewGate", true);
   228	    actionsTaken.push(`Enabled the stop-time review gate for ${workspaceRoot}.`);
   229	  } else if (options["disable-review-gate"]) {
   230	    setConfig(workspaceRoot, "stopReviewGate", false);
   231	    actionsTaken.push(`Disabled the stop-time review gate for ${workspaceRoot}.`);
   232	  }
   233	
   234	  const finalReport = buildSetupReport(cwd, actionsTaken);
   235	  outputResult(options.json ? finalReport : renderSetupReport(finalReport), options.json);
   236	}
   237	
   238	function buildAdversarialReviewPrompt(context, focusText) {
   239	  const template = loadPromptTemplate(ROOT_DIR, "adversarial-review");
   240	  return interpolateTemplate(template, {
   241	    REVIEW_KIND: "Adversarial Review",
   242	    TARGET_LABEL: context.target.label,
   243	    USER_FOCUS: focusText || "No extra focus provided.",
   244	    REVIEW_INPUT: context.content
   245	  });
   246	}
   247	
   248	function ensureCodexReady(cwd) {
   249	  const authStatus = getCodexLoginStatus(cwd);
   250	  if (!authStatus.available) {
   251	    throw new Error("Codex CLI is not installed or is missing required runtime support. Install it with `npm install -g @openai/codex`, then rerun `/codex:setup`.");
   252	  }
   253	  if (!authStatus.loggedIn) {
   254	    throw new Error("Codex CLI is not authenticated. Run `!codex login` and retry.");
   255	  }
   256	}
   257	
   258	function buildNativeReviewTarget(target) {
   259	  if (target.mode === "working-tree") {
   260	    return { type: "uncommittedChanges" };
   261	  }
   262	
   263	  if (target.mode === "branch") {
   264	    return { type: "baseBranch", branch: target.baseRef };
   265	  }
   266	
   267	  return null;
   268	}
   269	
   270	function validateNativeReviewRequest(target, focusText) {
   271	  if (focusText.trim()) {
   272	    throw new Error(
   273	      `\`/codex:review\` now maps directly to the built-in reviewer and does not support custom focus text. Retry with \`/codex:adversarial-review ${focusText.trim()}\` for focused review instructions.`
   274	    );
   275	  }
   276	
   277	  const nativeTarget = buildNativeReviewTarget(target);
   278	  if (!nativeTarget) {
   279	    throw new Error("This `/codex:review` target is not supported by the built-in reviewer. Retry with `/codex:adversarial-review` for custom targeting.");
   280	  }
   281	
   282	  return nativeTarget;
   283	}
   284	
   285	function renderStatusPayload(report, asJson) {
   286	  return asJson ? report : renderStatusReport(report);
   287	}
   288	
   289	function isActiveJobStatus(status) {
   290	  return status === "queued" || status === "running";
   291	}
   292	
   293	async function waitForSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference, options = {}) {
   294	  const timeoutMs = Math.max(0, Number(options.timeoutMs) || DEFAULT_STATUS_WAIT_TIMEOUT_MS);
   295	  const pollIntervalMs = Math.max(100, Number(options.pollIntervalMs) || DEFAULT_STATUS_POLL_INTERVAL_MS);
   296	  const deadline = Date.now() + timeoutMs;
   297	  let snapshot = buildSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference);
   298	
   299	  while (isActiveJobStatus(snapshot.job.status) && Date.now() < deadline) {
   300	    await sleep(Math.min(pollIntervalMs, Math.max(0, deadline - Date.now())));
   301	    snapshot = buildSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference);
   302	  }
   303	
   304	  return {
   305	    ...snapshot,
   306	    waitTimedOut: isActiveJobStatus(snapshot.job.status),
   307	    timeoutMs
   308	  };
   309	}
   310	
   311	async function resolveLatestTrackedTaskThread(cwd, options = {}) {
   312	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   313	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(listJobs(workspaceRoot)).filter((job) => job.id !== options.excludeJobId);
   314	  const activeTask = jobs.find((job) => job.jobClass === "task" && (job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running"));
   315	  if (activeTask) {
   316	    throw new Error(`Task ${activeTask.id} is still running. Use /codex:status before continuing it.`);
   317	  }
   318	
   319	  const trackedTask = jobs.find((job) => job.jobClass === "task" && job.status === "completed" && job.threadId);
   320	  if (trackedTask) {
   321	    return { id: trackedTask.threadId };
   322	  }
   323	
   324	  return findLatestTaskThread(workspaceRoot);
   325	}
   326	
   327	async function executeReviewRun(request) {
   328	  ensureCodexReady(request.cwd);
   329	  ensureGitRepository(request.cwd);
   330	
   331	  const target = resolveReviewTarget(request.cwd, {
   332	    base: request.base,
   333	    scope: request.scope
   334	  });
   335	  const focusText = request.focusText?.trim() ?? "";
   336	  const reviewName = request.reviewName ?? "Review";
   337	  if (reviewName === "Review") {
   338	    const reviewTarget = validateNativeReviewRequest(target, focusText);
   339	    const result = await runAppServerReview(request.cwd, {
   340	      target: reviewTarget,
   341	      model: request.model,
   342	      onProgress: request.onProgress
   343	    });
   344	    const payload = {
   345	      review: reviewName,
   346	      target,
   347	      threadId: result.threadId,
   348	      sourceThreadId: result.sourceThreadId,
   349	      codex: {
   350	        status: result.status,
   351	        stderr: result.stderr,
   352	        stdout: result.reviewText,
   353	        reasoning: result.reasoningSummary
   354	      }
   355	    };
   356	    const rendered = renderNativeReviewResult(
   357	      {
   358	        status: result.status,
   359	        stdout: result.reviewText,
   360	        stderr: result.stderr
   361	      },
   362	      { reviewLabel: reviewName, targetLabel: target.label, reasoningSummary: result.reasoningSummary }
   363	    );
   364	
   365	    return {
   366	      exitStatus: result.status,
   367	      threadId: result.threadId,
   368	      turnId: result.turnId,
   369	      payload,
   370	      rendered,
   371	      summary: firstMeaningfulLine(result.reviewText, `${reviewName} completed.`),
   372	      jobTitle: `Codex ${reviewName}`,
   373	      jobClass: "review",
   374	      targetLabel: target.label
   375	    };
   376	  }
   377	
   378	  const context = collectReviewContext(request.cwd, target);
   379	  const prompt = buildAdversarialReviewPrompt(context, focusText);
   380	  const result = await runAppServerTurn(context.repoRoot, {
   381	    prompt,
   382	    model: request.model,
   383	    sandbox: "read-only",
   384	    outputSchema: readOutputSchema(REVIEW_SCHEMA),
   385	    onProgress: request.onProgress
   386	  });
   387	  const parsed = parseStructuredOutput(result.finalMessage, {
   388	    status: result.status,
   389	    failureMessage: result.error?.message ?? result.stderr
   390	  });
   391	  const payload = {
   392	    review: reviewName,
   393	    target,
   394	    threadId: result.threadId,
   395	    context: {
   396	      repoRoot: context.repoRoot,
   397	      branch: context.branch,
   398	      summary: context.summary
   399	    },
   400	    codex: {
   401	      status: result.status,
   402	      stderr: result.stderr,
   403	      stdout: result.finalMessage,
   404	      reasoning: result.reasoningSummary
   405	    },
   406	    result: parsed.parsed,
   407	    rawOutput: parsed.rawOutput,
   408	    parseError: parsed.parseError,
   409	    reasoningSummary: result.reasoningSummary
   410	  };
   411	
   412	  return {
   413	    exitStatus: result.status,
   414	    threadId: result.threadId,
   415	    turnId: result.turnId,
   416	    payload,
   417	    rendered: renderReviewResult(parsed, {
   418	      reviewLabel: reviewName,
   419	      targetLabel: context.target.label,
   420	      reasoningSummary: result.reasoningSummary
   421	    }),
   422	    summary: parsed.parsed?.summary ?? parsed.parseError ?? firstMeaningfulLine(result.finalMessage, `${reviewName} finished.`),
   423	    jobTitle: `Codex ${reviewName}`,
   424	    jobClass: "review",
   425	    targetLabel: context.target.label
   426	  };
   427	}

   429	
   430	async function executeTaskRun(request) {
   431	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(request.cwd);
   432	  ensureCodexReady(request.cwd);
   433	
   434	  const taskMetadata = buildTaskRunMetadata({
   435	    prompt: request.prompt,
   436	    resumeLast: request.resumeLast
   437	  });
   438	
   439	  let resumeThreadId = null;
   440	  if (request.resumeLast) {
   441	    const latestThread = await resolveLatestTrackedTaskThread(workspaceRoot, {
   442	      excludeJobId: request.jobId
   443	    });
   444	    if (!latestThread) {
   445	      throw new Error("No previous Codex task thread was found for this repository.");
   446	    }
   447	    resumeThreadId = latestThread.id;
   448	  }
   449	
   450	  if (!request.prompt && !resumeThreadId) {
   451	    throw new Error("Provide a prompt, a prompt file, piped stdin, or use --resume-last.");
   452	  }
   453	
   454	  const result = await runAppServerTurn(workspaceRoot, {
   455	    resumeThreadId,
   456	    prompt: request.prompt,
   457	    defaultPrompt: resumeThreadId ? DEFAULT_CONTINUE_PROMPT : "",
   458	    model: request.model,
   459	    effort: request.effort,
   460	    sandbox: request.write ? "workspace-write" : "read-only",
   461	    onProgress: request.onProgress,
   462	    persistThread: true,
   463	    threadName: resumeThreadId ? null : buildPersistentTaskThreadName(request.prompt || DEFAULT_CONTINUE_PROMPT)
   464	  });
   465	
   466	  const rawOutput = typeof result.finalMessage === "string" ? result.finalMessage : "";
   467	  const failureMessage = result.error?.message ?? result.stderr ?? "";
   468	  const rendered = renderTaskResult(
   469	    {
   470	      rawOutput,
   471	      failureMessage,
   472	      reasoningSummary: result.reasoningSummary
   473	    },
   474	    {
   475	      title: taskMetadata.title,
   476	      jobId: request.jobId ?? null,
   477	      write: Boolean(request.write)
   478	    }
   479	  );
   480	  const payload = {
   481	    status: result.status,
   482	    threadId: result.threadId,
   483	    rawOutput,
   484	    touchedFiles: result.touchedFiles,
   485	    reasoningSummary: result.reasoningSummary
   486	  };
   487	
   488	  return {
   489	    exitStatus: result.status,
   490	    threadId: result.threadId,
   491	    turnId: result.turnId,
   492	    payload,
   493	    rendered,
   494	    summary: firstMeaningfulLine(rawOutput, firstMeaningfulLine(failureMessage, `${taskMetadata.title} finished.`)),
   495	    jobTitle: taskMetadata.title,
   496	    jobClass: "task",
   497	    write: Boolean(request.write)
   498	  };
   499	}
   500	
   501	function buildReviewJobMetadata(reviewName, target) {
   502	  return {
   503	    kind: reviewName === "Adversarial Review" ? "adversarial-review" : "review",
   504	    title: reviewName === "Review" ? "Codex Review" : `Codex ${reviewName}`,
   505	    summary: `${reviewName} ${target.label}`
   506	  };
   507	}

   961	async function main() {
   962	  const [subcommand, ...argv] = process.argv.slice(2);
   963	  if (!subcommand || subcommand === "help" || subcommand === "--help") {
   964	    printUsage();
   965	    return;
   966	  }
   967

   970	      handleSetup(argv);
   971	      break;
   972	    case "review":
   973	      await handleReview(argv);
   974	      break;

   978	      });

   311	async function resolveLatestTrackedTaskThread(cwd, options = {}) {
   312	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   313	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(listJobs(workspaceRoot)).filter((job) => job.id !== options.excludeJobId);
   314	  const activeTask = jobs.find((job) => job.jobClass === "task" && (job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running"));
   315	  if (activeTask) {
   316	    throw new Error(`Task ${activeTask.id} is still running. Use /codex:status before continuing it.`);
   317	  }
   318	
   319	  const trackedTask = jobs.find((job) => job.jobClass === "task" && job.status === "completed" && job.threadId);
   320	  if (trackedTask) {
   321	    return { id: trackedTask.threadId };
   322	  }
   323	
   324	  return findLatestTaskThread(workspaceRoot);
   325	}

   767	async function handleTaskWorker(argv) {
   768	  const { options } = parseCommandInput(argv, {
   769	    valueOptions: ["cwd", "job-id"]
   770	  });
   771	
   772	  if (!options["job-id"]) {
   773	    throw new Error("Missing required --job-id for task-worker.");
   774	  }
   775	
   776	  const cwd = resolveCommandCwd(options);
   777	  const workspaceRoot = resolveCommandWorkspace(options);
   778	  const storedJob = readStoredJob(workspaceRoot, options["job-id"]);
   779	  if (!storedJob) {
   780	    throw new Error(`No stored job found for ${options["job-id"]}.`);
   781	  }
   782	
   783	  const request = storedJob.request;
   784	  if (!request || typeof request !== "object") {
   785	    throw new Error(`Stored job ${options["job-id"]} is missing its task request payload.`);
   786	  }
   787	
   788	  const { logFile, progress } = createTrackedProgress(
   789	    {
   790	      ...storedJob,
   791	      workspaceRoot
   792	    },
   793	    {
   794	      logFile: storedJob.logFile ?? null
   795	    }
   796	  );
   797	  await runTrackedJob(
   798	    {
   799	      ...storedJob,
   800	      workspaceRoot,
   801	      logFile
   802	    },
   803	    () =>
   804	      executeTaskRun({
   805	        ...request,
   806	        onProgress: progress
   807	      }),
   808	    { logFile }
   809	  );
   810	}

   812	async function handleStatus(argv) {
   813	  const { options, positionals } = parseCommandInput(argv, {
   814	    valueOptions: ["cwd", "timeout-ms", "poll-interval-ms"],
   815	    booleanOptions: ["json", "all", "wait"]
   816	  });
   817	
   818	  const cwd = resolveCommandCwd(options);
   819	  const reference = positionals[0] ?? "";
   820	  if (reference) {
   821	    const snapshot = options.wait
   822	      ? await waitForSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference, {
   823	          timeoutMs: options["timeout-ms"],
   824	          pollIntervalMs: options["poll-interval-ms"]
   825	        })
   826	      : buildSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference);
   827	    outputCommandResult(snapshot, renderJobStatusReport(snapshot.job), options.json);
   828	    return;
   829	  }
   830	
   831	  if (options.wait) {
   832	    throw new Error("`status --wait` requires a job id.");
   833	  }
   834	
   835	  const report = buildStatusSnapshot(cwd, { all: options.all });
   836	  outputResult(renderStatusPayload(report, options.json), options.json);
   837	}

   704	async function handleTask(argv) {
   705	  const { options, positionals } = parseCommandInput(argv, {
   706	    valueOptions: ["model", "effort", "cwd", "prompt-file"],
   707	    booleanOptions: ["json", "write", "resume-last", "resume", "fresh", "background"],
   708	    aliasMap: {
   709	      m: "model"
   710	    }
   711	  });
   712	
   713	  const cwd = resolveCommandCwd(options);
   714	  const workspaceRoot = resolveCommandWorkspace(options);
   715	  const model = normalizeRequestedModel(options.model);
   716	  const effort = normalizeReasoningEffort(options.effort);
   717	  const prompt = readTaskPrompt(cwd, options, positionals);
   718	
   719	  const resumeLast = Boolean(options["resume-last"] || options.resume);
   720	  const fresh = Boolean(options.fresh);
   721	  if (resumeLast && fresh) {
   722	    throw new Error("Choose either --resume/--resume-last or --fresh.");
   723	  }
   724	  const write = Boolean(options.write);
   725	  const taskMetadata = buildTaskRunMetadata({
   726	    prompt,
   727	    resumeLast
   728	  });
   729	
   730	  if (options.background) {
   731	    ensureCodexReady(cwd);
   732	    requireTaskRequest(prompt, resumeLast);
   733	
   734	    const job = buildTaskJob(workspaceRoot, taskMetadata, write);
   735	    const request = buildTaskRequest({
   736	      cwd,
   737	      model,
   738	      effort,
   739	      prompt,
   740	      write,
   741	      resumeLast,
   742	      jobId: job.id
   743	    });
   744	    const { payload } = enqueueBackgroundTask(cwd, job, request);
   745	    outputCommandResult(payload, renderQueuedTaskLaunch(payload), options.json);
   746	    return;
   747	  }
   748	
   749	  const job = buildTaskJob(workspaceRoot, taskMetadata, write);
   750	  await runForegroundCommand(
   751	    job,
   752	    (progress) =>
   753	      executeTaskRun({
   754	        cwd,
   755	        model,
   756	        effort,
   757	        prompt,
   758	        write,
   759	        resumeLast,
   760	        jobId: job.id,
   761	        onProgress: progress
   762	      }),
   763	    { json: options.json }
   764	  );
   765	}

   896	export async function findLatestTaskThread(cwd) {
   897	  const availability = getCodexAvailability(cwd);
   898	  if (!availability.available) {
   899	    throw new Error("Codex CLI is not installed or is missing required runtime support. Install it with `npm install -g @openai/codex`, then rerun `/codex:setup`.");
   900	  }
   901	
   902	  return withAppServer(cwd, async (client) => {
   903	    const response = await client.request("thread/list", {
   904	      cwd,
   905	      limit: 20,
   906	      sortKey: "updated_at",
   907	      sourceKinds: ["appServer"],
   908	      searchTerm: TASK_THREAD_PREFIX
   909	    });
   910	
   911	    return (
   912	      response.data.find((thread) => typeof thread.name === "string" && thread.name.startsWith(TASK_THREAD_PREFIX)) ??
   913	      null
   914	    );
   915	  });
   916	}

    12	function normalizeProgressEvent(value) {
    13	  if (value && typeof value === "object" && !Array.isArray(value)) {
    14	    return {
    15	      message: String(value.message ?? "").trim(),
    16	      phase: typeof value.phase === "string" && value.phase.trim() ? value.phase.trim() : null,
    17	      threadId: typeof value.threadId === "string" && value.threadId.trim() ? value.threadId.trim() : null,
    18	      turnId: typeof value.turnId === "string" && value.turnId.trim() ? value.turnId.trim() : null,
    19	      stderrMessage: value.stderrMessage == null ? null : String(value.stderrMessage).trim(),
    20	      logTitle: typeof value.logTitle === "string" && value.logTitle.trim() ? value.logTitle.trim() : null,
    21	      logBody: value.logBody == null ? null : String(value.logBody).trimEnd()
    22	    };
    23	  }
    24	
    25	  return {
    26	    message: String(value ?? "").trim(),
    27	    phase: null,
    28	    threadId: null,
    29	    turnId: null,
    30	    stderrMessage: String(value ?? "").trim(),
    31	    logTitle: null,
    32	    logBody: null
    33	  };
    34	}

    36	export function appendLogLine(logFile, message) {
    37	  const normalized = String(message ?? "").trim();
    38	  if (!logFile || !normalized) {
    39	    return;
    40	  }
    41	  fs.appendFileSync(logFile, `[${nowIso()}] ${normalized}\n`, "utf8");
    42	}
    43	
    44	export function appendLogBlock(logFile, title, body) {
    45	  if (!logFile || !body) {
    46	    return;
    47	  }
    48	  fs.appendFileSync(logFile, `\n[${nowIso()}] ${title}\n${String(body).trimEnd()}\n`, "utf8");
    49	}

    51	export function createJobLogFile(workspaceRoot, jobId, title) {
    52	  const logFile = resolveJobLogFile(workspaceRoot, jobId);
    53	  fs.writeFileSync(logFile, "", "utf8");
    54	  if (title) {
    55	    appendLogLine(logFile, `Starting ${title}.`);
    56	  }
    57	  return logFile;
    58	}

    60	export function createJobRecord(base, options = {}) {
    61	  const env = options.env ?? process.env;
    62	  const sessionId = env[options.sessionIdEnv ?? SESSION_ID_ENV];
    63	  return {
    64	    ...base,
    65	    createdAt: nowIso(),

    67	  };

    70	export function createJobProgressUpdater(workspaceRoot, jobId) {
    71	  let lastPhase = null;
    72	  let lastThreadId = null;
    73	  let lastTurnId = null;
    74	
    75	  return (event) => {
    76	    const normalized = normalizeProgressEvent(event);
    77	    const patch = { id: jobId };
    78	    let changed = false;
    79	
    80	    if (normalized.phase && normalized.phase !== lastPhase) {
    81	      lastPhase = normalized.phase;
    82	      patch.phase = normalized.phase;
    83	      changed = true;
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    if (normalized.threadId && normalized.threadId !== lastThreadId) {
    87	      lastThreadId = normalized.threadId;
    88	      patch.threadId = normalized.threadId;
    89	      changed = true;
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    if (normalized.turnId && normalized.turnId !== lastTurnId) {
    93	      lastTurnId = normalized.turnId;
    94	      patch.turnId = normalized.turnId;
    95	      changed = true;
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    if (!changed) {
    99	      return;
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    upsertJob(workspaceRoot, patch);
   103	
   104	    const jobFile = resolveJobFile(workspaceRoot, jobId);
   105	    if (!fs.existsSync(jobFile)) {
   106	      return;
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    const storedJob = readJobFile(jobFile);
   110	    writeJobFile(workspaceRoot, jobId, {
   111	      ...storedJob,
   112	      ...patch
   113	    });
   114	  };
   115	}
   116	
   117	export function createProgressReporter({ stderr = false, logFile = null, onEvent = null } = {}) {
   118	  if (!stderr && !logFile && !onEvent) {
   119	    return null;
   120	  }
   121	
   122	  return (eventOrMessage) => {
   123	    const event = normalizeProgressEvent(eventOrMessage);
   124	    const stderrMessage = event.stderrMessage ?? event.message;
   125	    if (stderr && stderrMessage) {
   126	      process.stderr.write(`[codex] ${stderrMessage}\n`);
   127	    }
   128	    appendLogLine(logFile, event.message);
   129	    appendLogBlock(logFile, event.logTitle, event.logBody);
   130	    onEvent?.(event);
   131	  };
   132	}
   133	
   134	function readStoredJobOrNull(workspaceRoot, jobId) {
   135	  const jobFile = resolveJobFile(workspaceRoot, jobId);
   136	  if (!fs.existsSync(jobFile)) {
   137	    return null;
   138	  }
   139	  return readJobFile(jobFile);
   140	}
   141	
   142	export async function runTrackedJob(job, runner, options = {}) {
   143	  const runningRecord = {
   144	    ...job,
   145	    status: "running",
   146	    startedAt: nowIso(),
   147	    phase: "starting",
   148	    pid: process.pid,
   149	    logFile: options.logFile ?? job.logFile ?? null
   150	  };
   151	  writeJobFile(job.workspaceRoot, job.id, runningRecord);
   152	  upsertJob(job.workspaceRoot, runningRecord);
   153	
   154	  try {
   155	    const execution = await runner();
   156	    const completionStatus = execution.exitStatus === 0 ? "completed" : "failed";
   157	    const completedAt = nowIso();
   158	    writeJobFile(job.workspaceRoot, job.id, {
   159	      ...runningRecord,
   160	      status: completionStatus,
   161	      threadId: execution.threadId ?? null,
   162	      turnId: execution.turnId ?? null,
   163	      pid: null,
   164	      phase: completionStatus === "completed" ? "done" : "failed",
   165	      completedAt,
   166	      result: execution.payload,
   167	      rendered: execution.rendered
   168	    });
   169	    upsertJob(job.workspaceRoot, {
   170	      id: job.id,
   171	      status: completionStatus,
   172	      threadId: execution.threadId ?? null,
   173	      turnId: execution.turnId ?? null,
   174	      summary: execution.summary,
   175	      phase: completionStatus === "completed" ? "done" : "failed",
   176	      pid: null,
   177	      completedAt
   178	    });
   179	    appendLogBlock(options.logFile ?? job.logFile ?? null, "Final output", execution.rendered);
   180	    return execution;
   181	  } catch (error) {
   182	    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error);
   183	    const existing = readStoredJobOrNull(job.workspaceRoot, job.id) ?? runningRecord;
   184	    const completedAt = nowIso();
   185	    writeJobFile(job.workspaceRoot, job.id, {
   186	      ...existing,
   187	      status: "failed",
   188	      phase: "failed",
   189	      errorMessage,
   190	      pid: null,
   191	      completedAt,
   192	      logFile: options.logFile ?? job.logFile ?? existing.logFile ?? null
   193	    });
   194	    upsertJob(job.workspaceRoot, {
   195	      id: job.id,
   196	      status: "failed",
   197	      phase: "failed",
   198	      pid: null,
   199	      errorMessage,
   200	      completedAt
   201	    });
   202	    throw error;
   203	  }
   204	}

    49	function stripLogPrefix(line) {
    50	  return line.replace(/^\[[^\]]+\]\s*/, "").trim();
    51	}

    53	function isProgressBlockTitle(line) {
    54	  return (
    55	    ["Final output", "Assistant message", "Reasoning summary", "Review output"].includes(line) ||
    56	    /^Subagent .+ message$/.test(line) ||
    57	    /^Subagent .+ reasoning summary$/.test(line)
    58	  );
    59	}

    61	export function readJobProgressPreview(logFile, maxLines = DEFAULT_MAX_PROGRESS_LINES) {
    62	  if (!logFile || !fs.existsSync(logFile)) {
    63	    return [];
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  const lines = fs
    67	    .readFileSync(logFile, "utf8")
    68	    .split(/\r?\n/)
    69	    .map((line) => line.trimEnd())
    70	    .filter(Boolean)
    71	    .filter((line) => line.startsWith("["))
    72	    .map(stripLogPrefix)
    73	    .filter((line) => line && !isProgressBlockTitle(line));
    74	
    75	  return lines.slice(-maxLines);
    76	}
    77	
    78	function formatElapsedDuration(startValue, endValue = null) {
    79	  const start = Date.parse(startValue ?? "");
    80	  if (!Number.isFinite(start)) {
    81	    return null;
    82	  }
    83	
    84	  const end = endValue ? Date.parse(endValue) : Date.now();
    85	  if (!Number.isFinite(end) || end < start) {
    86	    return null;
    87	  }
    88	
    89	  const totalSeconds = Math.max(0, Math.round((end - start) / 1000));
    90	  const hours = Math.floor(totalSeconds / 3600);
    91	  const minutes = Math.floor((totalSeconds % 3600) / 60);
    92	  const seconds = totalSeconds % 60;
    93	
    94	  if (hours > 0) {
    95	    return `${hours}h ${minutes}m`;
    96	  }
    97	  if (minutes > 0) {
    98	    return `${minutes}m ${seconds}s`;
    99	  }
   100	  return `${seconds}s`;
   101	}
   102	
   103	function looksLikeVerificationCommand(line) {
   104	  return /\b(test|tests|lint|build|typecheck|type-check|check|verify|validate|pytest|jest|vitest|cargo test|npm test|pnpm test|yarn test|go test|mvn test|gradle test|tsc|eslint|ruff)\b/i.test(
   105	    line
   106	  );
   107	}
   108	
   109	function inferLegacyJobPhase(job, progressPreview = []) {
   110	  switch (job.status) {
   111	    case "queued":
   112	      return "queued";
   113	    case "cancelled":
   114	      return "cancelled";
   115	    case "failed":
   116	      return "failed";
   117	    case "completed":
   118	      return "done";
   119	    default:
   120	      break;
   121	  }
   122	
   123	  for (let index = progressPreview.length - 1; index >= 0; index -= 1) {
   124	    const line = progressPreview[index].toLowerCase();
   125	    if (line.startsWith("starting codex") || line.startsWith("thread ready") || line.startsWith("turn started")) {
   126	      return "starting";
   127	    }
   128	    if (line.startsWith("reviewer started") || line.includes("review mode")) {
   129	      return "reviewing";
   130	    }
   131	    if (line.startsWith("searching:") || line.startsWith("calling ") || line.startsWith("running tool:")) {
   132	      return "investigating";
   133	    }
   134	    if (line.startsWith("starting collaboration tool:")) {
   135	      return "investigating";
   136	    }
   137	    if (line.startsWith("running command:")) {
   138	      return looksLikeVerificationCommand(line)
   139	        ? "verifying"
   140	        : job.jobClass === "review"
   141	          ? "reviewing"
   142	          : "investigating";
   143	    }
   144	    if (line.startsWith("command completed:")) {
   145	      return looksLikeVerificationCommand(line) ? "verifying" : "running";
   146	    }
   147	    if (line.startsWith("applying ") || line.startsWith("file changes ")) {
   148	      return "editing";
   149	    }
   150	    if (line.startsWith("turn completed")) {
   151	      return "finalizing";
   152	    }
   153	    if (line.startsWith("codex error:") || line.startsWith("failed:")) {
   154	      return "failed";
   155	    }
   156	  }
   157	
   158	  return job.jobClass === "review" ? "reviewing" : "running";
   159	}
   160	
   161	export function enrichJob(job, options = {}) {
   162	  const maxProgressLines = options.maxProgressLines ?? DEFAULT_MAX_PROGRESS_LINES;
   163	  const enriched = {
   164	    ...job,
   165	    kindLabel: getJobTypeLabel(job),
   166	    progressPreview:
   167	      job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running" || job.status === "failed"
   168	        ? readJobProgressPreview(job.logFile, maxProgressLines)
   169	        : [],
   170	    elapsed: formatElapsedDuration(job.startedAt ?? job.createdAt, job.completedAt ?? null),
   171	    duration:
   172	      job.status === "completed" || job.status === "failed" || job.status === "cancelled"
   173	        ? formatElapsedDuration(job.startedAt ?? job.createdAt, job.completedAt ?? job.updatedAt)
   174	        : null
   175	  };
   176	
   177	  return {
   178	    ...enriched,
   179	    phase: enriched.phase ?? inferLegacyJobPhase(enriched, enriched.progressPreview)
   180	  };
   181	}
   182	
   183	export function readStoredJob(workspaceRoot, jobId) {
   184	  const jobFile = resolveJobFile(workspaceRoot, jobId);
   185	  if (!fs.existsSync(jobFile)) {
   186	    return null;
   187	  }
   188	  return readJobFile(jobFile);
   189	}
   190	
   191	function matchJobReference(jobs, reference, predicate = () => true) {
   192	  const filtered = jobs.filter(predicate);
   193	  if (!reference) {
   194	    return filtered[0] ?? null;
   195	  }
   196	
   197	  const exact = filtered.find((job) => job.id === reference);
   198	  if (exact) {
   199	    return exact;
   200	  }
   201	
   202	  const prefixMatches = filtered.filter((job) => job.id.startsWith(reference));
   203	  if (prefixMatches.length === 1) {
   204	    return prefixMatches[0];
   205	  }
   206	  if (prefixMatches.length > 1) {
   207	    throw new Error(`Job reference "${reference}" is ambiguous. Use a longer job id.`);
   208	  }
   209	
   210	  throw new Error(`No job found for "${reference}". Run /codex:status to list known jobs.`);
   211	}
   212	
   213	export function buildStatusSnapshot(cwd, options = {}) {
   214	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   215	  const config = getConfig(workspaceRoot);
   216	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(filterJobsForCurrentSession(listJobs(workspaceRoot), options));
   217	  const maxJobs = options.maxJobs ?? DEFAULT_MAX_STATUS_JOBS;
   218	  const maxProgressLines = options.maxProgressLines ?? DEFAULT_MAX_PROGRESS_LINES;
   219	
   220	  const running = jobs
   221	    .filter((job) => job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running")
   222	    .map((job) => enrichJob(job, { maxProgressLines }));
   223	
   224	  const latestFinishedRaw = jobs.find((job) => job.status !== "queued" && job.status !== "running") ?? null;
   225	  const latestFinished = latestFinishedRaw ? enrichJob(latestFinishedRaw, { maxProgressLines }) : null;
   226	
   227	  const recent = (options.all ? jobs : jobs.slice(0, maxJobs))
   228	    .filter((job) => job.status !== "queued" && job.status !== "running" && job.id !== latestFinished?.id)
   229	    .map((job) => enrichJob(job, { maxProgressLines }));
   230	
   231	  return {
   232	    workspaceRoot,
   233	    config,
   234	    sessionRuntime: getSessionRuntimeStatus(options.env),
   235	    running,
   236	    latestFinished,
   237	    recent,
   238	    needsReview: Boolean(config.stopReviewGate)
   239	  };
   240	}
   241	
   242	export function buildSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference, options = {}) {
   243	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   244	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(listJobs(workspaceRoot));
   245	  const selected = matchJobReference(jobs, reference);
   246	  if (!selected) {
   247	    throw new Error(`No job found for "${reference}". Run /codex:status to inspect known jobs.`);
   248	  }
   249	
   250	  return {
   251	    workspaceRoot,
   252	    job: enrichJob(selected, { maxProgressLines: options.maxProgressLines })
   253	  };
   254	}
   255	
   256	export function resolveResultJob(cwd, reference) {
   257	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   258	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(reference ? listJobs(workspaceRoot) : filterJobsForCurrentSession(listJobs(workspaceRoot)));
   259	  const selected = matchJobReference(
   260	    jobs,
   261	    reference,
   262	    (job) => job.status === "completed" || job.status === "failed" || job.status === "cancelled"
   263	  );
   264	
   265	  if (selected) {
   266	    return { workspaceRoot, job: selected };
   267	  }
   268	
   269	  const active = matchJobReference(jobs, reference, (job) => job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running");
   270	  if (active) {
   271	    throw new Error(`Job ${active.id} is still ${active.status}. Check /codex:status and try again once it finishes.`);
   272	  }
   273	
   274	  if (reference) {
   275	    throw new Error(`No finished job found for "${reference}". Run /codex:status to inspect active jobs.`);
   276	  }
   277	
   278	  throw new Error("No finished Codex jobs found for this repository yet.");
   279	}
   280	
   281	export function resolveCancelableJob(cwd, reference) {
   282	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   283	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(listJobs(workspaceRoot));
   284	  const activeJobs = jobs.filter((job) => job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running");
   285	
   286	  if (reference) {
   287	    const selected = matchJobReference(activeJobs, reference);
   288	    if (!selected) {
   289	      throw new Error(`No active job found for "${reference}".`);
   290	    }
   291	    return { workspaceRoot, job: selected };
   292	  }
   293	
   294	  if (activeJobs.length === 1) {
   295	    return { workspaceRoot, job: activeJobs[0] };
   296	  }
   297	  if (activeJobs.length > 1) {
   298	    throw new Error("Multiple Codex jobs are active. Pass a job id to /codex:cancel.");
   299	  }
   300	
   301	  throw new Error("No active Codex jobs to cancel.");
   302	}
   303

   549	function createTrackedProgress(job, options = {}) {
   550	  const logFile = options.logFile ?? createJobLogFile(job.workspaceRoot, job.id, job.title);
   551	  return {
   552	    logFile,
   553	    progress: createProgressReporter({

   557	    })
   558	  };
   559	}

   573	function buildTaskRequest({ cwd, model, effort, prompt, write, resumeLast, jobId }) {
   574	  return {
   575	    cwd,
   576	    model,
   577	    effort,
   578	    prompt,
   579	    write,

   581	    jobId

   585	function readTaskPrompt(cwd, options, positionals) {
   586	  if (options["prompt-file"]) {
   587	    return fs.readFileSync(path.resolve(cwd, options["prompt-file"]), "utf8");
   588	  }
   589	
   590	  const positionalPrompt = positionals.join(" ");
   591	  return positionalPrompt || readStdinIfPiped();
   592	}
   593	
   594	function requireTaskRequest(prompt, resumeLast) {
   595	  if (!prompt && !resumeLast) {
   596	    throw new Error("Provide a prompt, a prompt file, piped stdin, or use --resume-last.");
   597	  }
   598	}
   599	
   600	async function runForegroundCommand(job, runner, options = {}) {
   601	  const { logFile, progress } = createTrackedProgress(job, {
   602	    logFile: options.logFile,
   603	    stderr: !options.json
   604	  });
   605	  const execution = await runTrackedJob(job, () => runner(progress), { logFile });
   606	  outputResult(options.json ? execution.payload : execution.rendered, options.json);
   607	  if (execution.exitStatus !== 0) {
   608	    process.exitCode = execution.exitStatus;
   609	  }
   610	  return execution;
   611	}
   612	
   613	function spawnDetachedTaskWorker(cwd, jobId) {
   614	  const scriptPath = path.join(ROOT_DIR, "scripts", "codex-companion.mjs");
   615	  const child = spawn(process.execPath, [scriptPath, "task-worker", "--cwd", cwd, "--job-id", jobId], {
   616	    cwd,
   617	    env: process.env,
   618	    detached: true,
   619	    stdio: "ignore",
   620	    windowsHide: true
   621	  });
   622	  child.unref();
   623	  return child;
   624	}
   625	
   626	function enqueueBackgroundTask(cwd, job, request) {
   627	  const { logFile } = createTrackedProgress(job);
   628	  appendLogLine(logFile, "Queued for background execution.");
   629	
   630	  const child = spawnDetachedTaskWorker(cwd, job.id);
   631	  const queuedRecord = {
   632	    ...job,
   633	    status: "queued",
   634	    phase: "queued",
   635	    pid: child.pid ?? null,
   636	    logFile,
   637	    request
   638	  };
   639	  writeJobFile(job.workspaceRoot, job.id, queuedRecord);
   640	  upsertJob(job.workspaceRoot, queuedRecord);
   641	
   642	  return {
   643	    payload: {
   644	      jobId: job.id,
   645	      status: "queued",
   646	      title: job.title,
   647	      summary: job.summary,
   648	      logFile
   649	    },
   650	    logFile
   651	  };
   652	}

import fs from "node:fs";
import path from "node:path";
import { execSync } from "node:child_process";

const ROOT = "/testbed";
const SCRIPT = path.join(ROOT, "plugins/codex/scripts/codex-companion.mjs");

function makeTempDir() {
  return fs.mkdtempSync(path.join("/tmp", "test-repro-"));
}

// We need to reproduce: a workspace with state that has a completed task from sess-other
// Then run task-resume-candidate with sess-current -> should say available: false
// Then run task --resume-last with sess-current -> currently will still find the other session's task

// To do this properly, we need to use the CLI itself with appropriate env vars
// Let's create a workspace and use the CLI to create state

const workspace = makeTempDir();
const pluginDataDir = makeTempDir();

// First, let's initialize git repo
execSync("git init", { cwd: workspace, encoding: "utf8" });
execSync("git config user.email test@test.com", { cwd: workspace, encoding: "utf8" });
execSync("git config user.name Test", { cwd: workspace, encoding: "utf8" });
execSync("git commit --allow-empty -m init", { cwd: workspace, encoding: "utf8" });

// Run setup to initialize state
const envBase = { ...process.env, CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DATA: pluginDataDir };

// Now, we need to simulate a completed task from sess-other. 
// Since we can't actually run Codex, we'll create the state manually.

import { resolveStateDir, listJobs, writeJobFile } from "./plugins/codex/scripts/lib/state.mjs";

const stateDir = resolveStateDir(workspace);
console.log("stateDir:", stateDir);

const jobId = "task-sess-other-001";

  id: jobId,
  status: "completed",
  title: "Codex Task",
  jobClass: "task",
  sessionId: "sess-other",
  threadId: "thr_other",
  summary: "Old task from other session",
  updatedAt: "2026-03-24T20:05:00.000Z",
  createdAt: "2026-03-24T20:00:00.000Z"
}, null, 2), "utf8");

// Also create a state.json file

  version: 1,

    id: jobId,
    status: "completed",
    title: "Codex Task",
    jobClass: "task",
    sessionId: "sess-other",
    threadId: "thr_other",
    summary: "Old task from other session",
    updatedAt: "2026-03-24T20:05:00.000Z",
    createdAt: "2026-03-24T20:00:00.000Z"
  }]
};

  const result = execSync(`node ${SCRIPT} task-resume-candidate --json`, {
    cwd: workspace,
    encoding: "utf8",
    env: { ...envBase, CODEX_COMPANION_SESSION_ID: "sess-current" }
  });
  console.log("stdout:", result.trim());

  console.log("available:", payload.available, "(expected: false)");
} catch (e) {
  console.log("Error:", e.message);
}

// Test 2: task-resume-candidate with sess-other

try {

     1	import { createHash } from "node:crypto";
     2	import fs from "node:fs";
     3	import os from "node:os";
     4	import path from "node:path";
     5	
     6	import { resolveWorkspaceRoot } from "./workspace.mjs";
     7	
     8	const STATE_VERSION = 1;
     9	const PLUGIN_DATA_ENV = "CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DATA";
    10	const FALLBACK_STATE_ROOT_DIR = path.join(os.tmpdir(), "codex-companion");
    11	const STATE_FILE_NAME = "state.json";
    12	const JOBS_DIR_NAME = "jobs";
    13	const MAX_JOBS = 50;
    14	
    15	function nowIso() {
    16	  return new Date().toISOString();
    17	}
    18	
    19	function defaultState() {
    20	  return {
    21	    version: STATE_VERSION,
    22	    config: {
    23	      stopReviewGate: false
    24	    },
    25	    jobs: []
    26	  };
    27	}
    28	
    29	export function resolveStateDir(cwd) {
    30	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
    31	  let canonicalWorkspaceRoot = workspaceRoot;
    32	  try {
    33	    canonicalWorkspaceRoot = fs.realpathSync.native(workspaceRoot);
    34	  } catch {
    35	    canonicalWorkspaceRoot = workspaceRoot;
    36	  }
    37	
    38	  const slugSource = path.basename(workspaceRoot) || "workspace";
    39	  const slug = slugSource.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/g, "-").replace(/^-+|-+$/g, "") || "workspace";
    40	  const hash = createHash("sha256").update(canonicalWorkspaceRoot).digest("hex").slice(0, 16);
    41	  const pluginDataDir = process.env[PLUGIN_DATA_ENV];
    42	  const stateRoot = pluginDataDir ? path.join(pluginDataDir, "state") : FALLBACK_STATE_ROOT_DIR;
    43	  return path.join(stateRoot, `${slug}-${hash}`);
    44	}
    45	
    46	export function resolveStateFile(cwd) {
    47	  return path.join(resolveStateDir(cwd), STATE_FILE_NAME);
    48	}
    49	
    50	export function resolveJobsDir(cwd) {
    51	  return path.join(resolveStateDir(cwd), JOBS_DIR_NAME);
    52	}
    53	
    54	export function ensureStateDir(cwd) {
    55	  fs.mkdirSync(resolveJobsDir(cwd), { recursive: true });
    56	}
    57	
    58	export function loadState(cwd) {
    59	  const stateFile = resolveStateFile(cwd);
    60	  if (!fs.existsSync(stateFile)) {
    61	    return defaultState();
    62	  }
    63	
    64	  try {
    65	    const parsed = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(stateFile, "utf8"));
    66	    return {
    67	      ...defaultState(),
    68	      ...parsed,
    69	      config: {
    70	        ...defaultState().config,
    71	        ...(parsed.config ?? {})
    72	      },
    73	      jobs: Array.isArray(parsed.jobs) ? parsed.jobs : []
    74	    };
    75	  } catch {
    76	    return defaultState();
    77	  }
    78	}
    79	
    80	function pruneJobs(jobs) {
    81	  return [...jobs]
    82	    .sort((left, right) => String(right.updatedAt ?? "").localeCompare(String(left.updatedAt ?? "")))
    83	    .slice(0, MAX_JOBS);
    84	}
    85	
    86	function removeFileIfExists(filePath) {
    87	  if (filePath && fs.existsSync(filePath)) {
    88	    fs.unlinkSync(filePath);
    89	  }
    90	}
    91	
    92	export function saveState(cwd, state) {
    93	  const previousJobs = loadState(cwd).jobs;
    94	  ensureStateDir(cwd);
    95	  const nextJobs = pruneJobs(state.jobs ?? []);
    96	  const nextState = {
    97	    version: STATE_VERSION,
    98	    config: {
    99	      ...defaultState().config,
   100	      ...(state.config ?? {})
   101	    },
   102	    jobs: nextJobs
   103	  };
   104	
   105	  const retainedIds = new Set(nextJobs.map((job) => job.id));
   106	  for (const job of previousJobs) {
   107	    if (retainedIds.has(job.id)) {
   108	      continue;
   109	    }
   110	    removeJobFile(resolveJobFile(cwd, job.id));
   111	    removeFileIfExists(job.logFile);
   112	  }
   113	
   114	  fs.writeFileSync(resolveStateFile(cwd), `${JSON.stringify(nextState, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8");
   115	  return nextState;
   116	}
   117	
   118	export function updateState(cwd, mutate) {
   119	  const state = loadState(cwd);
   120	  mutate(state);
   121	  return saveState(cwd, state);
   122	}
   123	
   124	export function generateJobId(prefix = "job") {
   125	  const random = Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8);
   126	  return `${prefix}-${Date.now().toString(36)}-${random}`;
   127	}
   128	
   129	export function upsertJob(cwd, jobPatch) {
   130	  return updateState(cwd, (state) => {
   131	    const timestamp = nowIso();
   132	    const existingIndex = state.jobs.findIndex((job) => job.id === jobPatch.id);
   133	    if (existingIndex === -1) {
   134	      state.jobs.unshift({
   135	        createdAt: timestamp,
   136	        updatedAt: timestamp,
   137	        ...jobPatch
   138	      });
   139	      return;
   140	    }
   141	    state.jobs[existingIndex] = {
   142	      ...state.jobs[existingIndex],
   143	      ...jobPatch,
   144	      updatedAt: timestamp
   145	    };
   146	  });
   147	}
   148	
   149	export function listJobs(cwd) {
   150	  return loadState(cwd).jobs;
   151	}
   152	
   153	export function setConfig(cwd, key, value) {
   154	  return updateState(cwd, (state) => {
   155	    state.config = {
   156	      ...state.config,
   157	      [key]: value
   158	    };
   159	  });
   160	}
   161	
   162	export function getConfig(cwd) {
   163	  return loadState(cwd).config;
   164	}
   165	
   166	export function writeJobFile(cwd, jobId, payload) {
   167	  ensureStateDir(cwd);
   168	  const jobFile = resolveJobFile(cwd, jobId);
   169	  fs.writeFileSync(jobFile, `${JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8");
   170	  return jobFile;
   171	}
   172	
   173	export function readJobFile(jobFile) {
   174	  return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(jobFile, "utf8"));
   175	}
   176	
   177	function removeJobFile(jobFile) {
   178	  if (fs.existsSync(jobFile)) {
   179	    fs.unlinkSync(jobFile);
   180	  }
   181	}
   182	
   183	export function resolveJobLogFile(cwd, jobId) {
   184	  ensureStateDir(cwd);
   185	  return path.join(resolveJobsDir(cwd), `${jobId}.log`);
   186	}
   187	
   188	export function resolveJobFile(cwd, jobId) {
   189	  ensureStateDir(cwd);
   190	  return path.join(resolveJobsDir(cwd), `${jobId}.json`);
   191	}

const ROOT = "/testbed";

function makeTempDir() {
  return fs.mkdtempSync(path.join("/tmp", "test-repro-"));
}

const workspace = makeTempDir();

// Initialize git repo

execSync("git config user.email test@test.com", { cwd: workspace, encoding: "utf8" });

Looking at the code again:

```javascript
async function resolveLatestTrackedTaskThread(cwd, options = {}) {
  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(listJobs(workspaceRoot)).filter((job) => job.id !== options.excludeJobId);
  const activeTask = jobs.find((job) => job.jobClass === "task" && (job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running"));
  if (activeTask) {
    throw new Error(`Task ${activeTask.id} is still running. Use /codex:status before continuing it.`);
  }

  const trackedTask = jobs.find((job) => job.jobClass === "task" && job.status === "completed" && job.threadId);
  if (trackedTask) {
    return { id: trackedTask.threadId };
  }

  return findLatestTaskThread(workspaceRoot);
}
```

The fix should:
1. Get the session ID from env (like `handleTaskResumeCandidate` does)
2. Filter jobs by session ID when present
3. Only check for active tasks within the same session
4. Only find completed tasks within the same session  
5. Only fall back to `findLatestTaskThread` when there's no session ID (since `findLatestTaskThread` queries the Codex app server directly and isn't session-scoped)

Let me now implement the fix

Good, all existing tests pass. Now let me think about edge cases:

1. **No session ID set**: The behavior should be unchanged - it should scan all jobs and fall back to `findLatestTaskThread`. Our code does this correctly because `if (sessionId)` guards the filtering.

2. **Session ID set, but no jobs with that session ID**: It returns `null`, which causes the "No previous Codex task thread was found" error. This is the desired behavior.

3. **Session ID set, but only active (running/queued) tasks from current session**: The active task check is properly scoped. If there's a running task from the current session, it will block (which is correct). If there's a running task from another session, it won't block (because it's filtered out).

4. **Session ID set, completed task from current session exists**: Returns the thread ID.

5. **Session ID set, multiple completed tasks from current session**: The `sortJobsNewestFirst` and `find` will pick the newest one.

Let me also verify that the `findLatestTaskThread` fallback is only called when there's no session ID. This is important because `findLatestTaskThread` queries the Codex app server directly and could return threads from other sessions.

    16	const STOP_REVIEW_TIMEOUT_MS = 15 * 60 * 1000;
    17	const SCRIPT_DIR = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
    18	const ROOT_DIR = path.resolve(SCRIPT_DIR, "..");
    19	const STOP_REVIEW_TASK_MARKER = "Run a stop-gate review of the previous Claude turn.";
    20	
    21	function readHookInput() {
    22	  const raw = fs.readFileSync(0, "utf8").trim();
    23	  if (!raw) {
    24	    return {};
    25	  }
    26	  return JSON.parse(raw);
    27	}
    28	
    29	function emitDecision(payload) {
    30	  process.stdout.write(`${JSON.stringify(payload)}\n`);
    31	}
    32	
    33	function logNote(message) {
    34	  if (!message) {
    35	    return;
    36	  }
    37	  process.stderr.write(`${message}\n`);
    38	}
    39	
    40	function filterJobsForCurrentSession(jobs, input = {}) {
    41	  const sessionId = input.session_id || process.env[SESSION_ID_ENV] || null;
    42	  if (!sessionId) {
    43	    return jobs;
    44	  }
    45	  return jobs.filter((job) => job.sessionId === sessionId);
    46	}
    47	
    48	function buildStopReviewPrompt(input = {}) {
    49	  const lastAssistantMessage = String(input.last_assistant_message ?? "").trim();
    50	  const template = loadPromptTemplate(ROOT_DIR, "stop-review-gate");
    51	  const claudeResponseBlock = lastAssistantMessage
    52	    ? ["Previous Claude response:", lastAssistantMessage].join("\n")
    53	    : "";
    54	  return interpolateTemplate(template, {
    55	    CLAUDE_RESPONSE_BLOCK: claudeResponseBlock
    56	  });
    57	}
    58	
    59	function buildSetupNote(cwd) {
    60	  const authStatus = getCodexLoginStatus(cwd);
    61	  if (authStatus.available && authStatus.loggedIn) {
    62	    return null;
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  const detail = authStatus.detail ? ` ${authStatus.detail}.` : "";
    66	  return `Codex is not set up for the review gate.${detail} Run /codex:setup and, if needed, !codex login.`;
    67	}
    68	
    69	function parseStopReviewOutput(rawOutput) {
    70	  const text = String(rawOutput ?? "").trim();
    71	  if (!text) {
    72	    return {
    73	      ok: false,
    74	      reason:
    75	        "The stop-time Codex review task returned no final output. Run /codex:review --wait manually or bypass the gate."
    76	    };
    77	  }
    78	
    79	  const firstLine = text.split(/\r?\n/, 1)[0].trim();
    80	  if (firstLine.startsWith("ALLOW:")) {
    81	    return { ok: true, reason: null };
    82	  }
    83	  if (firstLine.startsWith("BLOCK:")) {
    84	    const reason = firstLine.slice("BLOCK:".length).trim() || text;
    85	    return {
    86	      ok: false,
    87	      reason: `Codex stop-time review found issues that still need fixes before ending the session: ${reason}`
    88	    };
    89	  }
    90	
    91	  return {
    92	    ok: false,
    93	    reason:
    94	      "The stop-time Codex review task returned an unexpected answer. Run /codex:review --wait manually or bypass the gate."
    95	  };
    96	}
    97	
    98	function runStopReview(cwd, input = {}) {
    99	  const scriptPath = path.join(SCRIPT_DIR, "codex-companion.mjs");
   100	  const prompt = buildStopReviewPrompt(input);
   101	  const childEnv = {
   102	    ...process.env,
   103	    ...(input.session_id ? { [SESSION_ID_ENV]: input.session_id } : {})
   104	  };
   105	  const result = spawnSync(process.execPath, [scriptPath, "task", "--json", prompt], {
   106	    cwd,
   107	    env: childEnv,
   108	    encoding: "utf8",
   109	    timeout: STOP_REVIEW_TIMEOUT_MS
   110	  });
   111	
   112	  if (result.error?.code === "ETIMEDOUT") {
   113	    return {
   114	      ok: false,
   115	      reason:
   116	        "The stop-time Codex review task timed out after 15 minutes. Run /codex:review --wait manually or bypass the gate."
   117	    };
   118	  }
   119	
   120	  if (result.status !== 0) {
   121	    const detail = String(result.stderr || result.stdout || "").trim();
   122	    return {
   123	      ok: false,
   124	      reason: detail
   125	        ? `The stop-time Codex review task failed: ${detail}`
   126	        : "The stop-time Codex review task failed. Run /codex:review --wait manually or bypass the gate."
   127	    };
   128	  }
   129	
   130	  try {
   131	    const payload = JSON.parse(result.stdout);
   132	    return parseStopReviewOutput(payload?.rawOutput);
   133	  } catch {
   134	    return {
   135	      ok: false,
   136	      reason:
   137	        "The stop-time Codex review task returned invalid JSON. Run /codex:review --wait manually or bypass the gate."
   138	    };
   139	  }
   140	}
   141	
   142	function main() {
   143	  const input = readHookInput();
   144	  const cwd = input.cwd || process.env.CLAUDE_PROJECT_DIR || process.cwd();
   145	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   146	  const config = getConfig(workspaceRoot);
   147	
   148	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(filterJobsForCurrentSession(listJobs(workspaceRoot), input));
   149	  const runningJob = jobs.find((job) => job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running");
   150	  const runningTaskNote = runningJob
   151	    ? `Codex task ${runningJob.id} is still running. Check /codex:status and use /codex:cancel ${runningJob.id} if you want to stop it before ending the session.`
   152	    : null;
   153	
   154	  if (!config.stopReviewGate) {
   155	    logNote(runningTaskNote);
   156	    return;
   157	  }
   158	
   159	  const setupNote = buildSetupNote(cwd);
   160	  if (setupNote) {
   161	    logNote(setupNote);
   162	    logNote(runningTaskNote);
   163	    return;
   164	  }
   165	
   166	  const review = runStopReview(cwd, input);
   167	  if (!review.ok) {
   168	    emitDecision({
   169	      decision: "block",
   170	      reason: runningTaskNote ? `${runningTaskNote} ${review.reason}` : review.reason
   171	    });
   172	    return;
   173	  }
   174	
   175	  logNote(runningTaskNote);
   176	}
   177	
   178	main();
   179

   312	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   313	  const sessionId = process.env[SESSION_ID_ENV] ?? null;
